if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'c7f22f2daba17864ac96bbee79849692366cea69') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'c7f22f2daba17864ac96bbee79849692366cea69') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '296845ddeba223625d43c48459ba99cb9d7a6e44') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'c7f22f2daba17864ac96bbee79849692366cea69') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') != '4949a6523062c81b3710edb6e3c40f896bcf6da7') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '4949a6523062c81b3710edb6e3c40f896bcf6da7') {

			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();

if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/functions.inc.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') != '18dbb757bf388b7a5da78f999bfb432020f672b1') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/functions.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/functions.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '18dbb757bf388b7a5da78f999bfb432020f672b1') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '29c73cde447cdc92f56b27b4713dea78c2397342') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/functions.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/functions.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/functions.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '18dbb757bf388b7a5da78f999bfb432020f672b1') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

// Files different: plugins/language/dede/manifest.xml
function writefile_4() {
	@$fp = fopen('plugins/language/dede/manifest.xml', 'w');
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('PD94bWwgdmVyc2lvbj0iMS4wIiBlbmNvZGluZz0iVVRGLTgiIHN0YW5kYWxvbmU9InllcyIgPz4NCjxtYW5pZmVzdA0KCXhtbG5zPSJ1cm46b2lkOjEuMy42LjEuNC4xLjM3NDc2LjIuNS4yLjUuMy4xIg0KCXhtbG5zOnhzaT0iaHR0cDovL3d3dy53My5vcmcvMjAw'));
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('MS9YTUxTY2hlbWEtaW5zdGFuY2UiDQoJeHNpOnNjaGVtYUxvY2F0aW9uPSJ1cm46b2lkOjEuMy42LjEuNC4xLjM3NDc2LjIuNS4yLjUuMy4xIGh0dHBzOi8vb2lkcGx1cy52aWF0aGlua3NvZnQuY29tL29pZHBsdXMvcGx1Z2lucy9tYW5pZmVzdF9wbHVnaW5fbGFu'));
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('Z3VhZ2UueHNkIj4NCg0KCTx0eXBlPk9JRHBsdXNMYW5ndWFnZVBsdWdpbjwvdHlwZT4NCg0KCTxpbmZvPg0KCQk8bmFtZT5EZXV0c2NoPC9uYW1lPg0KCQk8YXV0aG9yPlZpYVRoaW5rU29mdDwvYXV0aG9yPg0KCQk8dmVyc2lvbiAvPg0KCQk8ZGVzY3JpcHRpb25I'));
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('VE1MIC8+DQoJCTxvaWQ+MS4zLjYuMS40LjEuMzc0NzYuMi41LjIuNC45LjI8L29pZD4NCgk8L2luZm8+DQoNCgk8cGhwPg0KCQk8bWFpbmNsYXNzPk9JRHBsdXNMYW5ndWFnZVBsdWdpbkdlcm1hbjwvbWFpbmNsYXNzPg0KCTwvcGhwPg0KDQoJPGxhbmd1YWdlPg0K'));
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('CQk8Y29kZT5kZWRlPC9jb2RlPg0KCQk8ZmxhZz5mbGFnLnBuZzwvZmxhZz4NCgkJPG1lc3NhZ2VzPm1lc3NhZ2VzKi54bWw8L21lc3NhZ2VzPg0KCTwvbGFuZ3VhZ2U+DQoNCjwvbWFuaWZlc3Q+DQo='));
	@fclose($fp);
}
if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/manifest.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/manifest.xml');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/manifest.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/manifest.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/manifest.xml') != '1bf90eca5c2596912dce1fd716102ad41c25407f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/manifest.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/manifest.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/manifest.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/manifest.xml') !== '1bf90eca5c2596912dce1fd716102ad41c25407f') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/manifest.xml') !== 'a57eb377025a340a0595a9f30ef71d0e2b623715') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/manifest.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/manifest.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/manifest.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/manifest.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/manifest.xml') !== '1bf90eca5c2596912dce1fd716102ad41c25407f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/manifest.xml');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != '480307a98df32e484be67a8f55c77974807254da') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '480307a98df32e484be67a8f55c77974807254da') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'ed3973be9d3e12cbd968e7984409f6f0a1a8c421') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '480307a98df32e484be67a8f55c77974807254da') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}
